<div id="searchBarMask"
     style="position: fixed; top: 0px; left: 0px; bottom: 0; right: 0; width: 100%; z-index: 101; height: 100%; display: none; background: rgb(0, 0, 0); opacity: 0"></div>
<script>window.__language = 'zh'</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
	(function() {
		try {
			var INTL_DOMAIN = 'intl.cloud.tencent.com';
			var CN_DOMAIN = 'cloud.tencent.com';
			var CN_DOMAIN_OLD = 'www.qcloud.com';
			var hostname = location.hostname;
			var syslang = navigator.language || navigator.browserLanguage || '';

			// 对初次访问的英文用户重定向到国际版
			if (document.cookie.search(/\bintl=[^;]/) == -1
				&& document.cookie.search(/\blanguage=[^;]/) == -1) {

				var redirectToIntlHomePattern = /^\/(?:solution)(?:$|\/)/;
				var redirectToIntlHostPattern = /^\/(?:$|home|document|product)(?:$|\/)/;

				if ((hostname == CN_DOMAIN || hostname == CN_DOMAIN_OLD) && syslang.indexOf('en') > -1) {
					// var replaceHostname = location.host.replace(/[^:]*/, INTL_DOMAIN);
					var replaceHostname = location.host;

					if (redirectToIntlHomePattern.test(location.pathname)) {
						location.href = location.protocol + '//' + replaceHostname + '?lang=en';
						return;
					}

					if (redirectToIntlHostPattern.test(location.pathname)) {
						var search = location.search;
						var destUrl = location.protocol + '//' + replaceHostname + location.pathname;

						// 如果本身url带有非法的lang或language参数时，需要做替换处理
						if (/lang(uage)?(=|$)/.test(search)) {
							search = location.search.replace(/&?lang(uage)?(=[^&]*|$)/g, '');
							search = search == '?' ? '' : search;
						}

						destUrl += search;

						if (destUrl.indexOf('?') != -1) {
							destUrl += '&lang=en';
						} else {
							destUrl += '?lang=en';
						}

						location.href = destUrl;
						return;
					}
				}
			}

		} catch (e) {console.warn(e)}
	})();
</script>
